# Factor Values
#
# The factor values allow any tile blocker to be dialled up or down, wherever.
#
# The values follow exponential growth. In testing a @tiny amount makes
# a blocker rare. And, for a modifier where a certain blocker is expected,
# @buckets ensures that even when the game produces the minimum amount of
# blockers on a planet there is a likelihood of the expected blocker appearing,
# so use @buckets sparingly.
#
# @enough is the middle value allowing three exponential magnitudes more than
# enough and three exponential magnitudes less than enough.
#
# These factor values intend to multiply a value of 10 therefore add = 10 is
# expected.

# Planet types and planet modifiers
@buckets = 12.8			# Use sparingly for planet modifiers that expect a certain
                    # tile blocker to appear for sure. Overuse will lead to
										# competing tile blockers and increased chance of a no show.
@loads = 6.4
@lot = 3.2
@enough = 1.6				# An average amount of tile blockers.
@some = 0.8
@little = 0.4
@tiny = 0.2					# A rare amount of tile blockers.
                    # Also used for a planet modifier reduction value.
@none = 0.0					# No tile blockers to appear.

# Planet modifiers only
@off = 1.0					# Used in draft to switch off a planet modifier as a
                    # multiple of 1.0 returns no change to add value. Comment
                    # out an @off line to reduce processing time when done.

# Base add value
@add_base = 10

cgm_pe_tile_blocker_spawn_table = {
	random_list = {
